## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / nonlinear oscillators
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. In nonlinear oscillator theory, the restoring force depends nonlinearly on displacement (e.g., cubic terms like Duffing oscillator), and damping may depend nonlinearly on velocity. The acceleration equation typically combines restoring forces, damping, and possibly driving terms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring force with linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring with linear damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping dependent on position)
- Driven oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (linear oscillator with sinusoidal driving)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven cubic nonlinear oscillator)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Quadratic damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (restoring force with quadratic velocity damping)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity-dependent damping)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (quadratic nonlinear restoring force)
- Combined nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * x**2 * v (mixed position-velocity nonlinearity)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x (time-modulated stiffness)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) â†’ symmetric potential wells, preserving oscillatory symmetry
- Even-power position terms (x**2) â†’ asymmetric potential, indicating broken symmetry in the restoring force
- Position-velocity cross terms (x**2 * v, x * v) â†’ amplitude-dependent damping or energy-dependent dissipation
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) â†’ external periodic driving force
- Negative linear coefficient with positive cubic coefficient (c0*x + c1*x**3 where c0<0, c1>0) â†’ double-well potential (Duffing-type bistability)
- Velocity terms proportional to (1 - x**2)*v â†’ self-sustained oscillations with limit cycle behavior (Van der Pol type)
- Pure position-dependent acceleration with no velocity terms â†’ conservative (Hamiltonian) system with energy conservation
- Odd powers of velocity (v, v**3) â†’ dissipative terms that respect time-reversal antisymmetry
